			<font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:16pt;">ADEPTUS HEALTH REPORTS </font><font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:16pt;">SECOND</font><font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:16pt;"> QUARTER </font><font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:16pt;">2015 </font><font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:16pt;">RESULTS</font><font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:16pt;"> AND RAISES FULL YEAR GUIDANCE</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:150%;text-align:center;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 16pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:16pt;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:14pt;">Systemwide Revenue Increased </font><font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:14pt;">136%</font><font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:14pt;">&nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:150%;text-align:center;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 14pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:14pt;">Net Operating Revenue Increased </font><font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:14pt;">103%</font><font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:14pt;">&nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:150%;text-align:center;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 14pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:14pt;">Adjusted EBITDA Increased </font><font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:14pt;">286%</font><font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:14pt;">&nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;text-align:center;color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">Lewisville, Texas (</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">July</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;"> 23, 2015) &#x2014; Adeptus Health&nbsp;Inc. (NYSE: ADPT) (&#x201C;ADPT&#x201D; or the &#x201C;Company&#x201D;), the largest operator of freestanding emergency rooms in the U.S., announced its results for the second quarter ended June 30, 2015. All comparisons included in this release are for the same period in the prior year, unless otherwise noted.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Second Quarter 2015 Highlights:</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<div style="width:100%"><table style="width:100%;" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0"><tr><td style="width:0pt;"><p style="width:0pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td valign="top" align="left" style="width: 18.00pt; display: inline;">
			<p style="color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:0pt;">
				<font style="margin:0pt;font-family:Symbol;color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-size:10pt;;"> &#xB7;</font>
			</p>
		</td><td style="width:0pt;"><p style="width:0pt;width:0pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td align="left" valign="top">
			<p style="color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:0pt;">
			<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;font-size:3pt;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">Systemwide net patient services revenue was </font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">$104.5</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;"> million versus </font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">$44.2</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;"> million in prior year, an increase of 136%;</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
		<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 0pt 13.2pt;text-indent: -13.2pt;color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<div style="width:100%"><table style="width:100%;" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0"><tr><td style="width:0pt;"><p style="width:0pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td valign="top" align="left" style="width: 18.00pt; display: inline;">
			<p style="color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:0pt;">
				<font style="margin:0pt;font-family:Symbol;color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-size:10pt;;"> &#xB7;</font>
			</p>
		</td><td style="width:0pt;"><p style="width:0pt;width:0pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td align="left" valign="top">
			<p style="color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:0pt;">
			<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">Net operating revenue was </font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">$89.6</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;"> million versus </font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">$44.2</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;"> million in prior year, an increase </font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">of </font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">103%</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">;</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
		<p style="margin:0pt;color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 0pt 13.2pt;text-indent: -13.2pt;color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Symbol;color:#000000;">&#xF0B7;</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;font-size:3pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">Adjusted EBITDA was </font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">$22.9</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;"> million versus </font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">$5.9</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;"> million in prior year, an increase of </font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">286%</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 0pt 13.2pt;text-indent: -13.2pt;color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 0pt 18pt;text-indent: -18pt;color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Symbol;color:#000000;">&#xF0B7;</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;font-size:3pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">Adjusted earnings per share was </font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">$0.44</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">and GAAP earnings per share </font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">was </font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">$0.97</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 0pt 18pt;text-indent: -18pt;color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 0pt 18pt;text-indent: -18pt;color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Symbol;color:#000000;">&#xF0B7;</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;font-size:3pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">Net income attributable to Adeptus Health Inc. was </font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">$10.6</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;"> million;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 0pt 18pt;text-indent: -18pt;color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 0pt 18pt;text-indent: -18pt;color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Symbol;color:#000000;">&#xF0B7;</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;font-size:3pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">Cash flow from operating activities was $13.0 million versus $0.3 million in prior year; and</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 0pt 18pt;text-indent: -18pt;color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 0pt 18pt;text-indent: -18pt;color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Symbol;color:#000000;">&#xF0B7;</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;font-size:3pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">The Company opened six</font><font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">freestanding facilities during the second quarter 2015</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 0pt 13.2pt;text-indent: -13.2pt;color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">2015 Guidance</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;color:#191919;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">Based on our strong performance in the second quarter of 2015 and continued full year growth plans including 24 freestanding facilities and two new hospitals, we are again raising guidance.&nbsp;&nbsp;We expect to generate systemwide net patient services revenue, which includes revenue from our unconsolidated joint ventures, of&nbsp;$400.0 million to $405.0 million&nbsp;for the full year 2015.&nbsp; We expect Adjusted EBITDA of&nbsp;$69.0</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;"> million</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;"> to $71.0 million and Adjusted</font><font style="display: inline;color:#191919;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">earnings per share of $1.10 to $1.15 for the full year 2015.&nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Results of Operations for the Second Quarter 2015</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">Thomas S. Hall, Chairman and CEO, stated, &#x201C;We are pleased with the second quarter results, which reflect our continued strong growth momentum. During the quarter, we opened six additional freestanding </font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">emergency rooms</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">, entered into a new partnership with University of Colorado Health and grew our existing partnership with Dignity Health in Arizona. As we continue to execute on our strategic plan,</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">both through expanding our network of freestanding emergency rooms and forging partnerships with leading healthcare providers, we are helping to transform the delivery of emergency care in the U</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">.</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">S.&#x201D;</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">So far this year, ADPT has opened 15 new facilities, including 12 freestanding emergency facilities in Texas and Colorado, and its first hospital and two freestanding emergency facilities in Arizona with partner, Dignity Health. In July, as part of its partnership with University of Colorado Health</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">,</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;"> its 13 freestanding emergency rooms in Colorado were rebranded as UC Health Emergency Room and construction began on two hospitals.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">

		</p>
		<p><font size="1"> </font></p><hr size="3" style="color:#999999" width="100%" align="center"></hr><p style="page-break-after:always">&nbsp;</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;;font-size: 10pt"><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">For the second quarter of 2015, ADPT generated total net operating revenue of </font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">$89.6</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;"> million, an increase of </font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">103%</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">.</font><a name="PB_1_120032_3020"></a><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;"> Net operating revenue exclude</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">s</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;"> revenue from 13 facilities in Colorado and the Arizona hospital and its freestanding facility, which are accounted for as equity method investments. The increase was primarily attributable to the impact of patient volumes from the expansion of the number of freestanding facilities</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;"> from 38 to 68 and annual gross charge increases.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;text-align:center;color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">Adjusted EBITDA increased </font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">286%</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;"> to </font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">$22.9</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;"> million. This increase was primarily attributable to a $45.4 million increase in net operating revenue, partially offset by increases in salaries, wages and benefits and other costs related to our growth initiatives. </font><font style="display: inline;">See "Non-GAAP Financial Measures Description and Reconciliation" and "Reconciliation of Adjusted EBITDA to Net Income (Loss)" below for further information related to Adjusted EBITDA and its reconciliation to net income (loss).</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">ADPT generated net </font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">income of </font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">$27.7</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">million for the quarter, of which </font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">$10.6</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;"> million</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;"> was attributable to Adeptus Health Inc., compared to a net loss of </font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">$9.4</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;"> million from the prior year, of which </font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">$2.0</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;"> million was attributable to Adeptus Health Inc. </font><font style="display: inline;">The increase in net income was due to an increase of $45.4 million in net operating revenue, coupled with a gain recognized on the contribution and change of control of previously owned freestanding facilities to the joint venture with University of Colorado Health.&nbsp;&nbsp;This increase was partially offset by </font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">increases in salaries, wages and benefits and other costs related to our growth initiatives and </font><font style="display: inline;">an increase in depreciation and amortization expense.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;">&nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;">Adjusted earnings per share was </font><font style="display: inline;">$0.44</font><font style="display: inline;"> per share and GAAP earnings per share </font><font style="display: inline;">was </font><font style="display: inline;">$0.97</font><font style="display: inline;"> per share for the quarter. Adjusted earnings per share is calculated using a weighted average of both Class A and Class B common shares outstanding, which was</font><font style="display: inline;"> an aggregate of</font><font style="display: inline;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;">20,766,094</font><font style="display: inline;"> common shares at June 30, 2015. Adjustments for the quarter include a $2</font><font style="display: inline;">4</font><font style="display: inline;">.</font><font style="display: inline;">3</font><font style="display: inline;"> million gain recognized on the contribution of existing freestanding facilities to the joint venture with University of Colorado Health, $2.0 million of preopening costs associated with new facility openings, $0.6 million of stock compensation expense, $1.0 million related to public offerings</font><font style="display: inline;"> of our Class A common stock</font><font style="display: inline;"> and $0.8 million of other costs associated with our growth initiatives and an adjustment for taxes in order to establish a normalized tax rate of 35% for comparability purposes. See "Non-GAAP Financial Measures Description and Reconciliation" and "Earnings Per Share Reconciliation" below for further information related to Adjusted earnings per share and its reconciliation to net income (loss).</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;">&nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Systemwide Financial Results</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;">&nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">For the second quarter of 2015, ADPT generated systemwide net patient services revenue of </font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">$104.5</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;"> million, an increase of </font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">136%</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">. The increase was primarily attributable to the impact of increased patient volumes from the expansion of the number of freestanding facilities from</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;"> 38 to 68, annual gross charge increases and the </font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">opening of the Dignity Health Arizona General Hospital, a full service general hospital located in Laveen, Arizona.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;">&nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">As of June 30, 2015, 13 freestanding facilities associated with our joint venture with University of Colorado Health and our Arizona hospital and its freestanding facility associated with our joint venture with Dignity Health were accounted for using the equity method. For consolidated subsidiaries, the Company&#x2019;s financial statements reflect 100% of the revenues and expenses for these subsidiaries, after elimination of intercompany transactions and accounts. For our unconsolidated joint ventures, consolidated statements of operations reflect those earnings in two line items:</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;">&nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<div style="width:100%"><table style="width:100%;" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0"><tr><td style="width:54pt;"><p style="width:54pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td valign="top" align="left" style="width: 18.00pt; display: inline;">
			<p style="color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:0pt;">
				<font style="margin:0pt;font-family:Symbol;color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-size:10pt;;"> &#xB7;</font>
			</p>
		</td><td style="width:0pt;"><p style="width:0pt;width:0pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td align="left" valign="top">
			<p style="color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:0pt;">
			<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">Equity in </font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">earnings</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;"> of unconsolidated joint ventures, which represents our share of the net income or loss of each equity method joint venture based on our ownership percentage; and</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
		<div style="width:100%"><table style="width:100%;" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0"><tr><td style="width:54pt;"><p style="width:54pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td valign="top" align="left" style="width: 18.00pt; display: inline;">
			<p style="color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:0pt;">
				<font style="margin:0pt;font-family:Symbol;color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-size:10pt;;"> &#xB7;</font>
			</p>
		</td><td style="width:0pt;"><p style="width:0pt;width:0pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td align="left" valign="top">
			<p style="color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:0pt;">
			<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">Management and contract services revenues, which represent the Company&#x2019;s combined income from management and contract services that are earned from managing the day-to-day operations and providing contract staffing of the facility.</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
		<p style="margin:0pt;color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">As a result of this accounting treatment in our reported results, management supplementally focuses on non-GAAP systemwide metrics to analyze the results of operations. These systemwide metrics include systemwide net patient services revenue. Systemwide metrics treat our unconsolidated facilities as if they were consolidated. While the revenues earned at the unconsolidated facilities are not recorded in our consolidated financial statements, management believes systemwide net patient services revenue growth is important to understand the Company&#x2019;s financial performance because it is used to interpret the sources of our growth and provide a growth metric incorporating the revenues earned by all affiliated facilities, regardless of the accounting treatment. As we execute on our strategy of partnering with health systems, management expects the number of our facilities accounted for under the equity method to increase relative to the total number of affiliated facilities.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Liquidity</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">At the end of the second quarter, the Company had cash of $46.1</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">million and $</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">9.5</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;"> million available under its revolv</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">ing</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;"> credit facility.&nbsp;&nbsp;Net cash flow from operation</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">s</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;"> was $13.0 million for the second quarter.&nbsp;&nbsp;Prior to the expiration of the delayed draw component of its credit facility, the Company borrowed an additional $30.0 million in the second quarter.&nbsp;&nbsp;At June 30, 2015, the Company had total long-term debt and capital lease obligations of $159.0 million and debt net of cash of $112.9 million.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;text-align:center;color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<a name="PB_2_120040_7748"></a><font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Market Outlook</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">

		</p>
		<p><font size="1"> </font></p><hr size="3" style="color:#999999" width="100%" align="center"></hr><p style="page-break-after:always">&nbsp;</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;;font-size: 10pt"><font style="display: inline;">&nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;">We are maintaining the growth of our freestanding emergency room network at an expected rate of opening 24 new sites per year, including both owned and joint venture facilities. Our second hospital, located in Carrollton, Texas, a Dallas-Ft Worth suburb, remains on schedule to open later this year.&nbsp; </font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;">&nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;">A</font><font style="display: inline;">DPT&#x2019;s</font><font style="display: inline;"> growth is addressing the </font><font style="display: inline;">shortage of</font><font style="display: inline;"> quality emergency medical&nbsp;care in the U.S. As the most recent American College of Emergency Physicians (ACEP) survey highlights, emergency visits are on the rise. Respondents noted that this rise is combined in part with an increase in the acuity of patients&#x2019; injuries and/or illnesses. Again, this underscores the growing need for additional access points to high quality, 24/7&nbsp;emergency care. Our facilities offer just that with convenient neighborhood locations.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;">&nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;">&#x201C;Our network of freestanding emergency rooms and partnerships with leading healthcare systems, such as Dignity Health and UC Health, provides us with flexibility in addressing the unmet need for expanded access to emergency medical care. We are continuously talking to other healthcare systems around the country about how we can help them bring improved access to the highest quality emergency care to the communities they serve,&#x201D; added Hall.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">

		<p style="margin:0pt;color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">About Adeptus Health Inc.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;">&nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;">Adeptus Health (NYSE:ADPT) is a leading patient-centered healthcare organization expanding access to the highest quality emergency medical care through its network of freestanding emergency rooms and partnerships with premier healthcare providers.&nbsp;&nbsp;In Texas, Adeptus Health owns and operates First Choice Emergency Room, the nation's largest and oldest network of independent freestanding emergency rooms. In Colorado, in partnership with University of Colorado Health, Adeptus Health operates UCHealth Emergency Rooms. In Arizona, with Dignity Health, the company owns and operates Dignity Health Arizona General Hospital and freestanding emergency rooms. All Adeptus Health freestanding facilities are fully equipped emergency rooms with a complete radiology suite of diagnostic technology (CT scanner, ultrasound, and digital X-ray), on-site laboratory, and staffed with board-certified physicians and emergency trained registered nurses. According to patient feedback collected by Press Ganey Associates Inc., Adeptus Health provides the highest quality emergency medical care and received the 2013 and 2014 Press Ganey Guardian of Excellence Award for exceeding the 95th percentile in patient satisfaction nationwide. For more information please visit us on the web at adhc.com.</font>
		</p>

			<font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Forward-Looking Statements</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">Certain statements and information herein may be deemed to be &#x201C;forward-looking statements&#x201D; within the meaning of the Federal Private Securities Litigation Reform Act of 1995. Forward-looking statements may include, but are not limited to, statements relating to our guidance, objectives, plans and strategies, and all statements (other than statements of historical facts) that address activities, events or developments that we intend, expect, project, believe or anticipate will or may occur in the future. Any forward-looking statements herein are made as of the date of this press release, and ADPT undertakes no duty to update or revise any such statements </font>
		</p>
		<p><font size="1"> </font></p><hr size="3" style="color:#999999" width="100%" align="center"></hr><p style="page-break-after:always">&nbsp;</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;;font-size: 10pt"><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">except as required by the federal securities laws. Forward-looking statements are not guarantees of future performance and are subject to risks and uncertainties. Important factors that could cause actual results, developments and business decisions to differ materially from forward-looking statements are described in ADPT&#x2019;s filings with the U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission (&#x201C;SEC&#x201D;) from time to time and which are accessible on the SEC&#x2019;s website at www.sec.gov, including in the section entitled &#x201C;Risk Factors&#x201D; in the Company&#x2019;s Form 10-K</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;"> for the fiscal year ended December 31, 2014</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">. Among the factors that could cause future results to differ materially from those provided in this press release are:</font><font style="display: inline;"> our ability to implement our growth strategy; our ability to maintain sufficient levels of cash flow to meet growth expectations; our ability to protect our brand; federal and state laws and regulations relating to our facilities, which could lead to the incurrence of significant penalties by us or require us to make significant changes to our operations; our ability to locate available facility sites on terms acceptable to us; competition from hospitals, clinics and other emergency care providers; our dependence on payments from third-party payors; our ability to source and procure new products and equipment to meet patient preferences; our reliance on Medical Properties Trust (&#x201C;MPT&#x201D;) and the MPT Master Funding and Development Agreement</font><font style="display: inline;">s</font><font style="display: inline;">; disruptions in the global financial markets leading to difficulty in borrowing sufficient amounts of capital to finance the carrying costs of inventory to pay for capital expenditures and operating costs; our ability or the ability of our healthcare system partners to negotiate favorable contracts or renew existing contracts with third-party payors on favorable terms; significant changes in our payor mix or case mix resulting from fluctuations in the types of cases treated at our facilities; </font><font style="display: inline;">significant changes in the rules, regulations and systems governing Medicare and Medicaid reimbursements; </font><font style="display: inline;">material changes in IRS revenue rulings, case law or the interpretation of such rulings; shortages of, or quality control issues with, emergency care-related products, equipment and medical supplies that could result in a disruption of our operations; the intense competition we face for patients, physician use of our facilities, strategic relationships and commercial payor contracts; the fact that we are subject to significant malpractice and related legal claims; the growth of patient receivables or the deterioration in the ability to collect on those accounts;</font><a name="A2220618Z424B4_HTM_PAGE_CM45501_1_52"></a><font style="display: inline;"> the impact on us of PPACA, which represents a significant change to the healthcare industry; and ensuring our continued compliance with HIPAA, which could require us to expend significant resources and capital;</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;"> and the factors discussed in the section entitled &#x201C;Risk Factors&#x201D; in the Company&#x2019;s Form 10-K</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;"> for the fiscal year ended December 31, 2014</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Non-GAAP Financial Measures Description and Reconciliation</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;">&nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">This press release includes presentations of Adjusted EBITDA, which is defined as net income before interest, taxes, depreciation and amortization, further adjusted to eliminate the impact of certain additional items, including, advisory services paid to our Sponsor, facility pre-opening expenses, management recruiting expenses, stock compensation expense and other non-recurring costs or gains.</font><a name="PB_4_120057_7608"></a>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;text-align:center;color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">This press release also includes presentation of Adjusted earnings (loss) per share, which is defined as earnings (loss) per share related to the Company&#x2019;s overall operation, including controlling and non-controlling interests, as adjusted to exclude certain additional items, including, advisory services paid to our Sponsor, facility preopening expenses, management recruiting expenses, stock compensation expense and other non-recurring costs </font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">or gains </font><font style="display: inline;">and an adjustment for taxes in order to establish a normalized tax rate of 35% for comparability purposes</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">, divided by the aggregate number of shares of Class A and Class B common stock outstanding as of the end of the period.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;">&nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">In addition, this press release presents systemwide metrics to analyze the results of operations. These systemwide metrics include systemwide net patient services revenue.&nbsp;&nbsp;Systemwide metrics treat our unconsolidated facilities as if they were consolidated. </font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;color:#000000;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;">&nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">These non-GAAP financial measures, Adjusted EBITDA, Adjusted earnings (loss) per share and systemwide metrics, are commonly used by management and investors as performance measures. The Company&#x2019;s non-GAAP financial measures are not considered measures of financial performance under U.S. generally accepted accounting principles (GAAP), and the items excluded therefrom are significant components in understanding and assessing our financial performance. These non-GAAP financial measures should not be considered in isolation or as an alternative to GAAP measures such as net income, cash flows provided by or used in operating, investing or financing activities or other financial statement data presented in our consolidated financial statements as an indicator of financial performance. Reconciliations of non-GAAP financial measures are provided in this press release.&nbsp; Since these non-GAAP financial measures are not measures determined in accordance with GAAP and are susceptible to varying calculations, these measures, as presented, may not be comparable to other similarly titled measures of other companies.</font>
		</p>
